msg:Traveling with a baby, I didn't expect it to be a stand-alone cottage with a yard when I booked it. The environment is super good. There is an independent pool in the yard. It is very convenient to play in the water with children when the weather is hot. The service staff are very enthusiastic, from the big brother who greets guests at the gate and manages the sightseeing car to the little sister who checks in. Everyone is very nice. They reminded us that there is no elevator on the way to the room and will help us send our luggage to the room. As a result, it was later discovered that it was the little sister at the front desk who sent it. She carried our two large boxes by herself, which made me embarrassed. The room is very large, the sanitary conditions are also very good, with an independent courtyard, and the room is not facing the street, so there is no need to worry about noise problems. The scenery and greening of the entire hotel are also very beautiful, and there is also its own artificial lake. If you get up early in the morning, it is also very good to walk around the hotel. It is really the first choice for leisure and vacation in Fuxian Lake!
